# Live TODO — Q3 to Q10000 (Sequential, No Jumping)

## Execution Rule

- Complete exactly one item at a time in numeric order (`Qn` before `Qn+1`).
- No jumping, no skipping, no parallel execution.
- For each item: implement slice -> run `npm run lint` + `npm run typecheck` -> mark `[x]` -> move to next.
- Current active item in this file: **Q3**
